{\footnotesize\ttfamily AWS\+\_\+\+TEST\+\_\+\+CASE\+\_\+\+FIXTURE (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{mqtt\+\_\+connection\+\_\+disconnect\+\_\+while\+\_\+reconnecting}]{,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{connection__state__test_8c_a7342c99fd1e030c166576b62464546f6}{s\+\_\+setup\+\_\+mqtt\+\_\+server\+\_\+fn}}}]{,  }\item[{s\+\_\+test\+\_\+mqtt\+\_\+connection\+\_\+disconnect\+\_\+while\+\_\+reconnecting}]{,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{connection__state__test_8c_a5aefdb096f8d66b08c8a82b6c8f1a66d}{s\+\_\+clean\+\_\+up\+\_\+mqtt\+\_\+server\+\_\+fn}}}]{,  }\item[{\&}]{test\+\_\+data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Regression test\+: Once upon a time there was a bug caused by race condition on the state of connection. The scenario is the server/broker closes the connection, while the client is making requests. The race condition between the eventloop thread closes the connection and the main thread makes request could cause a bug. Solution\+: put a lock for the state of connection, protect it from accessing by multiple threads at the same time. \mbox{\Hypertarget{connection__state__test_8c_a145fd5518f77651bdf72d01f01caafc2}\label{connection__state__test_8c_a145fd5518f77651bdf72d01f01caafc2}}
